\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename Derived$>$\newline
class Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base$<$ Derived $>$}
\doxylink{class_base}{Base} class for all dense matrices, vectors, and arrays 

This class is the base that is inherited by all dense objects (matrix, vector, arrays, and related expression types). The common \doxylink{namespace_eigen}{Eigen} API for dense objects is contained in this class.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em Derived} & is the derived type, e.\+g., a matrix type or an expression.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
This class can be extended with the help of the plugin mechanism described on the page \doxylink{TopicCustomizing_Plugins}{Extending Matrix\+Base (and other classes)} by defining the preprocessor symbol {\ttfamily EIGEN\+\_\+\+DENSEBASE\+\_\+\+PLUGIN}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\textbackslash{}blank \doxylink{TopicClassHierarchy}{The class hierarchy} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{PlainObject}{PlainObject}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ad871c3bef0abfc3673a6963d8201be21} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1internal_1_1conditional}{internal\+::conditional}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1internal_1_1is__same}{internal\+::is\+\_\+same}}$<$typenameinternal\+::traits$<$Derived$>$\+::\+Xpr\+Kind,\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_matrix_xpr}{Matrix\+Xpr}}$>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}},\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_aa301ef39d63443e9ef0b84f47350116e}{Plain\+Matrix}},\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a65328b7d6fc10a26ff6cd5801a6a44eb}{Plain\+Array}}$>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ae8396ff85d63082521e3324820df1009}{\+::type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Plain\+Object}



The plain matrix or array type corresponding to this expression. 

This is not necessarily exactly the return type of \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527}{eval()}. In the case of plain matrices, the return type of \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527}{eval()} is a const reference to a matrix, not a matrix! It is however guaranteed that the return type of \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527}{eval()} is either \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ad871c3bef0abfc3673a6963d8201be21}{Plain\+Object} or const \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ad871c3bef0abfc3673a6963d8201be21}{Plain\+Object}\&. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a14bb7d253c1de3a79db460c3d6371707}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!RandomAccessLinSpacedReturnType@{RandomAccessLinSpacedReturnType}}
\index{RandomAccessLinSpacedReturnType@{RandomAccessLinSpacedReturnType}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{RandomAccessLinSpacedReturnType}{RandomAccessLinSpacedReturnType}}

The type used to store indices 

This typedef is relevant for types that store multiple indices such as \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_permutation_matrix}{Permutation\+Matrix} or \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_transpositions}{Transpositions}, otherwise it defaults to \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Eigen\+::\+Index} \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\textbackslash{}blank \doxylink{TopicPreprocessorDirectives}{Preprocessor directives}, \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Eigen\+::\+Index}, \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base}{Sparse\+Matrix\+Base}.

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{MaxRowsAtCompileTime@{MaxRowsAtCompileTime}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!MaxRowsAtCompileTime@{MaxRowsAtCompileTime}}}\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a58b79dc273e900de443da04852a47d8fad2baadea085372837b0e80dc93be1306}\label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a58b79dc273e900de443da04852a47d8fad2baadea085372837b0e80dc93be1306} 
Max\+Rows\+At\+Compile\+Time&This value is equal to the maximum possible number of rows that this expression might have. If this expression might have an arbitrarily high number of rows, this value is set to {\itshape Dynamic}.

This value is useful to know when evaluating an expression, in order to determine whether it is possible to avoid doing a dynamic memory allocation.

This value is useful to know when evaluating an expression, in order to determine whether it is possible to avoid doing a dynamic memory allocation.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a58b79dc273e900de443da04852a47d8fa25cb495affdbd796198462b8ef06be91}{Size\+At\+Compile\+Time}, \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a58b79dc273e900de443da04852a47d8fad2baadea085372837b0e80dc93be1306}{Max\+Rows\+At\+Compile\+Time}, \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a58b79dc273e900de443da04852a47d8facc3a41000cf1d29dd1a320b2a09d2a65}{Max\+Cols\+At\+Compile\+Time} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{IsVectorAtCompileTime@{IsVectorAtCompileTime}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!IsVectorAtCompileTime@{IsVectorAtCompileTime}}}\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a58b79dc273e900de443da04852a47d8fa1156955c8099c5072934b74c72654ed0}\label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a58b79dc273e900de443da04852a47d8fa1156955c8099c5072934b74c72654ed0} 
Is\+Vector\+At\+Compile\+Time&This is set to true if either the number of rows or the number of columns is known at compile-\/time to be equal to 1. Indeed, in that case, we are dealing with a column-\/vector (if there is only one column) or with a row-\/vector (if there is only one row). \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Flags@{Flags}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!Flags@{Flags}}}\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a58b79dc273e900de443da04852a47d8fa7392c9b2ad41ba3c16fdc5306c04d581}\label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a58b79dc273e900de443da04852a47d8fa7392c9b2ad41ba3c16fdc5306c04d581} 
Flags&This stores expression \doxylink{group__flags}{Flags} flags which may or may not be inherited by new expressions constructed from this one. See the \doxylink{group__flags}{list of flags}. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{IsRowMajor@{IsRowMajor}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!IsRowMajor@{IsRowMajor}}}\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a58b79dc273e900de443da04852a47d8fa406b6af91d61d348ba1c9764bdd66008}\label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a58b79dc273e900de443da04852a47d8fa406b6af91d61d348ba1c9764bdd66008}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{_dense_base_8h_ad7f74cf0d006b06b945187535404355e}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL}} EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a73a0ff2ad5a52e67ea44242f9beb122a}{Block\+Xpr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_af7f922b73e3acdb4a430b72f1a1334a5}{\+::block}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{start\+Row}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{start\+Col}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{block\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{block\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a dynamic-\/size expression of a block in \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em start\+Row} & the first row in the block \\
\hline
{\em start\+Col} & the first column in the block \\
\hline

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Even though the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size matrix, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation. 
\end{DoxyNote}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} NRows, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} NCols$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{_dense_base_8h_ad7f74cf0d006b06b945187535404355e}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_dense_base_1_1_fixed_block_xpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ NRows, NCols $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{\+::\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_af7f922b73e3acdb4a430b72f1a1334a5}{\+::block}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{start\+Row}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{start\+Col}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{block\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{block\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a block in \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em NRows} & number of rows in block as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em NCols} & number of columns in block as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em start\+Row} & the first row in the block \\
\hline
{\em start\+Col} & the first column in the block \\
\hline
{\em block\+Rows} & number of rows in block as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em block\+Cols} & number of columns in block as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for blocks where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape block\+Rows} should equal {\itshape NRows} unless {\itshape NRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bottomRightCorner()}{bottomRightCorner()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a4da4017d3da32e349d0d9fccf9566a07} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CRows, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CCols$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{_dense_base_8h_ad7f74cf0d006b06b945187535404355e}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_dense_base_1_1_fixed_block_xpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ CRows, CCols $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{\+::\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::bottom\+Right\+Corner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{c\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{c\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a bottom-\/right corner of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em CRows} & number of rows in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em CCols} & number of columns in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em c\+Rows} & number of rows in corner as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em c\+Cols} & number of columns in corner as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for corners where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape c\+Rows} should equal {\itshape CRows} unless {\itshape CRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Constant()}{Constant()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a9053c1a2e9993febe50113b05aac0f20} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a3cb28fce3943b113439e17eef3c38552}{\+::\+Constant\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Constant (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a constant matrix of value {\itshape value} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
This variant is only for fixed-\/size \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base} types. For dynamic-\/size types, you need to use the variants taking size arguments.

The template parameter {\itshape Custom\+Nullary\+Op} is the type of the functor.

\index{Constant@{Constant}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Constant()}{Constant()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ab0ae1bfa72faedcaf53af81ca76c446b} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a3cb28fce3943b113439e17eef3c38552}{\+::\+Constant\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Constant (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{cols}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a constant matrix of value {\itshape value} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
The parameters {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} are the number of rows and of columns of the returned matrix. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base} type.

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size matrix types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} as arguments, so \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

The template parameter {\itshape Custom\+Nullary\+Op} is the type of the functor.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
class \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_cwise_nullary_op}{Cwise\+Nullary\+Op} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a3cb28fce3943b113439e17eef3c38552}{\+::\+Constant\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Constant (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{size}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a constant matrix of value {\itshape value} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
The parameter {\itshape size} is the size of the returned vector. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base} type.

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size vector types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape size} as argument, so \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

The template parameter {\itshape Custom\+Nullary\+Op} is the type of the functor.

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a70cf4c2bc191461b218771434807c7c5}{Eval\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::eval (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
the matrix or vector obtained by evaluating this expression.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Notice that in the case of a plain matrix or vector (not an expression) this function just returns a const reference, in order to avoid a useless copy.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
Be carefull with \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527}{eval()} and the auto C++ keyword, as detailed in this \doxylink{_topic_pitfalls_TopicPitfalls_auto_keyword}{page }. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a42519f2e9d1a0408ae119050971b4c0f}{Segment\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::head (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{n}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a dynamic-\/size expression of the first coefficients of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em n} & the number of coefficients in the segment\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Even though the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

a fixed-\/size expression of the first coefficients of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em N} & the number of coefficients in the segment as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em n} & the number of coefficients in the segment as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape n} should equal {\itshape N} unless {\itshape N} is {\itshape Dynamic}.

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a57c6f5516aa86d4c22f382f1a069a319}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!innerSize@{innerSize}}
\index{innerSize@{innerSize}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{innerSize()}{innerSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a57c6f5516aa86d4c22f382f1a069a319} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::inner\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
the inner size.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
For a vector, this is just the size. For a matrix (non-\/vector), this is the minor dimension with respect to the \doxylink{group___topic_storage_orders}{storage order}, i.\+e., the number of rows for a column-\/major matrix, and the number of columns for a row-\/major matrix. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a8848223bc635c9c10e7cc68ae343ad81}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!isApprox@{isApprox}}
\index{isApprox@{isApprox}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isApprox()}{isApprox()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a8848223bc635c9c10e7cc68ae343ad81} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::is\+Approx (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a25c2ae37392d553e4a75928c5d864470}{Real\+Scalar}} \&}]{prec}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
{\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is approximately equal to {\itshape other}, within the precision determined by {\itshape prec}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The fuzzy compares are done multiplicatively. Two vectors $ v $ and $ w $ are considered to be approximately equal within precision $ p $ if \[ \Vert v - w \Vert \leqslant p\,\min(\Vert v\Vert, \Vert w\Vert). \] For matrices, the comparison is done using the Hilbert-\/\+Schmidt norm (aka Frobenius norm L2 norm).

Because of the multiplicativeness of this comparison, one can\textquotesingle{}t use this function to check whether {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is approximately equal to the zero matrix or vector. Indeed, {\ttfamily is\+Approx(zero)} returns false unless {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} itself is exactly the zero matrix or vector. If you want to test whether {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is zero, use internal\+::is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than(const \+Real\+Scalar\&, Real\+Scalar) instead.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
internal\+::is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than(const Real\+Scalar\&, Real\+Scalar) const 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a7d61b8814a7547e88b25cba68b159f05}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!isMuchSmallerThan@{isMuchSmallerThan}}
\index{isMuchSmallerThan@{isMuchSmallerThan}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isMuchSmallerThan()}{isMuchSmallerThan()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a7d61b8814a7547e88b25cba68b159f05} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a25c2ae37392d553e4a75928c5d864470}{Real\+Scalar}} \&}]{prec}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
{\ttfamily true} if the norm of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is much smaller than the norm of {\itshape other}, within the precision determined by {\itshape prec}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The fuzzy compares are done multiplicatively. \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} vector $ v $ is considered to be much smaller than a vector $ w $ within precision $ p $ if \[ \Vert v \Vert \leqslant p\,\Vert w\Vert. \] For matrices, the comparison is done using the Hilbert-\/\+Schmidt norm.
\end{DoxyNote}

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a25c2ae37392d553e4a75928c5d864470}{Real\+Scalar}} \&}]{other}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a25c2ae37392d553e4a75928c5d864470}{Real\+Scalar}} \&}]{prec}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_num_traits}{Num\+Traits}}$<$~\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}}~$>$\+:\+:dummy\+\_\+precision()}}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_adfca6ff4e473f68fbbeabbd03b7504a9}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!isMuchSmallerThan@{isMuchSmallerThan}}
\index{isMuchSmallerThan@{isMuchSmallerThan}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isMuchSmallerThan()}{isMuchSmallerThan()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_adfca6ff4e473f68fbbeabbd03b7504a9} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::is\+Much\+Smaller\+Than (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const typename \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_num_traits}{Num\+Traits}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{boostmultiprec_8cpp_ad5abe8020ead32dcab5e3c15d6d7c30e}{\+::\+Real}} \&}]{other}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a25c2ae37392d553e4a75928c5d864470}{Real\+Scalar}} \&}]{prec}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
{\ttfamily true} if the norm of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is much smaller than {\itshape other}, within the precision determined by {\itshape prec}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The fuzzy compares are done multiplicatively. \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} vector $ v $ is considered to be much smaller than $ x $ within precision $ p $ if \[ \Vert v \Vert \leqslant p\,\vert x\vert. \]
\end{DoxyNote}
For matrices, the comparison is done using the Hilbert-\/\+Schmidt norm. For this reason, the value of the reference scalar {\itshape other} should come from the Hilbert-\/\+Schmidt norm of a reference matrix of same dimensions.

\index{LinSpaced@{LinSpaced}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{LinSpaced()}{LinSpaced()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a1dd502457286f60df1c3e90f9192c542} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a14bb7d253c1de3a79db460c3d6371707}{\+::\+Random\+Access\+Lin\+Spaced\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Lin\+Spaced (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{low}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{high}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Sets a linearly spaced vector.    

The function generates \textquotesingle{}size\textquotesingle{} equally spaced values in the closed interval \mbox{[}low,high\mbox{]}. When size is set to 1, a vector of length 1 containing \textquotesingle{}high\textquotesingle{} is returned.

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


For integer scalar types, an even spacing is possible if and only if the length of the range, i.\+e., {\ttfamily high-\/low} is a scalar multiple of {\ttfamily size-\/1}, or if {\ttfamily size} is a scalar multiple of the number of values {\ttfamily high-\/low+1} (meaning each value can be repeated the same number of time). If one of these two considions is not satisfied, then {\ttfamily high} is lowered to the largest value satisfying one of this constraint. Here are some examples\+:

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{NullaryExpr()}{NullaryExpr()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ace7d7f3237fde5e1a5c82d36c93685be} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Custom\+Nullary\+Op$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_cwise_nullary_op}{Cwise\+Nullary\+Op}}$<$ Custom\+Nullary\+Op, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ad871c3bef0abfc3673a6963d8201be21}{\+::\+Plain\+Object}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Nullary\+Expr (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{cols}{, }\item[{const Custom\+Nullary\+Op \&}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a matrix defined by a custom functor {\itshape func} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
The parameters {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} are the number of rows and of columns of the returned matrix. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix_base}{Matrix\+Base} type.

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size matrix types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} as arguments, so \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

The template parameter {\itshape Custom\+Nullary\+Op} is the type of the functor.

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Custom\+Nullary\+Op$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_cwise_nullary_op}{Cwise\+Nullary\+Op}}$<$ Custom\+Nullary\+Op, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ad871c3bef0abfc3673a6963d8201be21}{\+::\+Plain\+Object}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Nullary\+Expr (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{size}{, }\item[{const Custom\+Nullary\+Op \&}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a matrix defined by a custom functor {\itshape func} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
The parameter {\itshape size} is the size of the returned vector. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix_base}{Matrix\+Base} type.

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size vector types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape size} as argument, so \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

The template parameter {\itshape Custom\+Nullary\+Op} is the type of the functor.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_adb1ce2c904a1eb3f3bab81ced1b916b6} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a3cb28fce3943b113439e17eef3c38552}{\+::\+Constant\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Ones (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a matrix where all coefficients equal one.
\end{DoxyReturn}
The parameters {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} are the number of rows and of columns of the returned matrix. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix_base}{Matrix\+Base} type.

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size matrix types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} as arguments, so \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a1284a38971d817c33e40c226f6347e37}{Ones()} should be used instead.

\label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_MatrixBaseCommaInitRef}%
\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_MatrixBaseCommaInitRef}%
Convenient operator to set the coefficients of a matrix.

The coefficients must be provided in a row major order and exactly match the size of the matrix. Otherwise an assertion is raised.

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}

\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
According the c++ standard, the argument expressions of this comma initializer are evaluated in arbitrary order.

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC Derived \& \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::operator= (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base}{Eigen\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies the generic expression {\itshape other} into \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this. 

The expression must provide a (templated) eval\+To(\+Derived\& dst) const function which does the actual job. In practice, this allows any user to write its own special matrix without having to modify \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix_base}{Matrix\+Base}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a reference to \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ad78fff11f12aefa46318ae88b6efcc50}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!outerSize@{outerSize}}
\index{outerSize@{outerSize}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{outerSize()}{outerSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ad78fff11f12aefa46318ae88b6efcc50} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::outer\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
the outer size.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
For a vector, this returns just 1. For a matrix (non-\/vector), this is the major dimension with respect to the \doxylink{group___topic_storage_orders}{storage order}, i.\+e., the number of columns for a column-\/major matrix, and the number of rows for a row-\/major matrix. 
\end{DoxyNote}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a fixed-\/size random matrix or vector expression
\end{DoxyReturn}
\doxylink{example__custom__name_8cpp_a2c973620a3fe7f923747ed2baa1bae4e}{Numbers} are uniformly spread through their whole definition range for integer types, and in the \mbox{[}-\/1\+:1\mbox{]} range for floating point scalar types.

This variant is only for fixed-\/size \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix_base}{Matrix\+Base} types. For dynamic-\/size types, you need to use the variants taking size arguments.

\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


This expression has the "{}evaluate before nesting"{} flag so that it will be evaluated into a temporary matrix whenever it is nested in a larger expression. This prevents unexpected behavior with expressions involving random matrices.

\textbackslash{}not\+\_\+reentrant

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ae97f8d9d08f969c733c8144be6225756} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a050c96f67131df5e47e00c29446fb50d}{\+::\+Random\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Random (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a random matrix expression
\end{DoxyReturn}
\doxylink{example__custom__name_8cpp_a2c973620a3fe7f923747ed2baa1bae4e}{Numbers} are uniformly spread through their whole definition range for integer types, and in the \mbox{[}-\/1\+:1\mbox{]} range for floating point scalar types.

The parameters {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} are the number of rows and of columns of the returned matrix. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix_base}{Matrix\+Base} type.

\textbackslash{}not\+\_\+reentrant

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size matrix types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} as arguments, so \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ae814abb451b48ed872819192dc188c19}{Random()} should be used instead.

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


This expression has the "{}evaluate before nesting"{} flag so that it will be evaluated into a temporary matrix whenever it is nested in a larger expression. This prevents unexpected behavior with expressions involving random matrices.

See \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a08224b09985b372f108850b1c605feed}{Dense\+Base\+::\+Nullary\+Expr(\+Index, const Custom\+Nullary\+Op\&)} for an example using C++11 random generators.

The template parameter {\itshape Binary\+Op} is the type of the functor {\itshape func} which must be an associative operator. Both current C++98 and C++11 functor styles are handled.

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a13027a493a68a13496610caf3d81bd3e}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!resize@{resize}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{resize()}{resize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a13027a493a68a13496610caf3d81bd3e} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{new\+Size}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Only plain matrices/arrays, not expressions, may be resized; therefore the only useful resize methods are \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a99d9054ee2d5a40c6e00ded0265e9cea}{Matrix\+::resize()} and \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a99d9054ee2d5a40c6e00ded0265e9cea}{Array\+::resize()}. The present method only asserts that the new size equals the old size, and does nothing else. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_aef40c2ee48a85a799270c8258cc12b76}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!resize@{resize}}
\index{resize@{resize}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{resize()}{resize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_aef40c2ee48a85a799270c8258cc12b76} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Only plain matrices/arrays, not expressions, may be resized; therefore the only useful resize methods are \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a99d9054ee2d5a40c6e00ded0265e9cea}{Matrix\+::resize()} and \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a99d9054ee2d5a40c6e00ded0265e9cea}{Array\+::resize()}. The present method only asserts that the new size equals the old size, and does nothing else. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a38ea394036d8b096abf322469c80198f}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!reverse@{reverse}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ada2ea028e35de0beef990fa0f6e3dee1} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_af49b9a56cfe2d2dc02e18dc073bcfbfa}{Const\+Reverse\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::reverse (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

This is the const version of \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a38ea394036d8b096abf322469c80198f}{reverse()}. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_adb8045155ea45f7961fc2a5170e1d921}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!reverseInPlace@{reverseInPlace}}
\index{reverseInPlace@{reverseInPlace}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{reverseInPlace()}{reverseInPlace()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_adb8045155ea45f7961fc2a5170e1d921} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::reverse\+In\+Place (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

This is the "{}in place"{} version of reverse\+: it reverses {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}.

In most cases it is probably better to simply use the reversed expression of a matrix. However, when reversing the matrix data itself is really needed, then this "{}in-\/place"{} version is probably the right choice because it provides the following additional benefits\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item less error prone\+: doing the same operation with .\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a38ea394036d8b096abf322469c80198f}{reverse()} requires special care\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}.reverse().eval();\ }

\end{DoxyCode}

\item this API enables reverse operations without the need for a temporary
\item it allows future optimizations (cache friendliness, etc.)
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_vectorwise_op_ab9dd7c273eb2ba8defaab2d55156936b}{Vectorwise\+Op\+::reverse\+In\+Place()}, \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a38ea394036d8b096abf322469c80198f}{reverse()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
函数调用图\+:

\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Even though the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

template$<$typename Then\+Derived, typename Else\+Derived$>$ \\
const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_select}{Select}}$<$ Derived, Then\+Derived, Else\+Derived $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::select (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Then\+Derived $>$ \&}]{then\+Matrix}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Else\+Derived $>$ \&}]{else\+Matrix}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a matrix where each coefficient (i,j) is equal to {\itshape then\+Matrix(i,j)} if {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this}(i,j), and {\itshape else\+Matrix(i,j)} otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLinSpaced()}{setLinSpaced()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a99dd31774d69545aba5d4f598cd27c4b} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} Derived \& \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::set\+Lin\+Spaced (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{low}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5feed465b3a8e60c47e73ecce83e39a2}{Scalar}} \&}]{high}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets a linearly spaced vector. 

The function fills {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with equally spaced values in the closed interval \mbox{[}low,high\mbox{]}. When size is set to 1, a vector of length 1 containing \textquotesingle{}high\textquotesingle{} is returned.

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors

For integer scalar types, do not miss the explanations on the definition of \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a513c7986f48517c36f992a558f81e591}{even spacing }.

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_aec3cf8f4f73c641d21a2c080c3e59662}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!tail@{tail}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{tail()}{tail()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_aec3cf8f4f73c641d21a2c080c3e59662} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a42519f2e9d1a0408ae119050971b4c0f}{Segment\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::tail (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{n}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a dynamic-\/size expression of the last coefficients of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em n} & the number of coefficients in the segment\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Even though the returned expression has dynamic size, in the case when it is applied to a fixed-\/size vector, it inherits a fixed maximal size, which means that evaluating it does not cause a dynamic memory allocation.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{topLeftCorner()}{topLeftCorner()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_adf64562fbef632199b09418ae65dff79} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CRows, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CCols$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{_dense_base_8h_ad7f74cf0d006b06b945187535404355e}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_dense_base_1_1_fixed_block_xpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ CRows, CCols $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{\+::\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::top\+Left\+Corner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{c\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{c\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a top-\/left corner of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em CRows} & number of rows in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em CCols} & number of columns in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em c\+Rows} & number of rows in corner as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em c\+Cols} & number of columns in corner as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for corners where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape c\+Rows} should equal {\itshape CRows} unless {\itshape CRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

Example\+:

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}

template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CRows, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} CCols$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{_dense_base_8h_ad7f74cf0d006b06b945187535404355e}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+DOC\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+ADDONS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INNER\+\_\+\+PANEL}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_dense_base_1_1_fixed_block_xpr}{Fixed\+Block\+Xpr}}$<$ CRows, CCols $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{\+::\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::top\+Right\+Corner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{c\+Rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{c\+Cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a top-\/right corner of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em CRows} & number of rows in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
{\em CCols} & number of columns in corner as specified at compile-\/time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em c\+Rows} & number of rows in corner as specified at run-\/time \\
\hline
{\em c\+Cols} & number of columns in corner as specified at run-\/time\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is mainly useful for corners where the number of rows is specified at compile-\/time and the number of columns is specified at run-\/time, or vice versa. The compile-\/time and run-\/time information should not contradict. In other words, {\itshape c\+Rows} should equal {\itshape CRows} unless {\itshape CRows} is {\itshape Dynamic}, and the same for the number of columns.

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac8952c19644a4ac7e41bea45c19b909c}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!transpose@{transpose}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{transpose()}{transpose()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac8952c19644a4ac7e41bea45c19b909c} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_transpose}{Transpose}}$<$ Derived $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abddae8e27995e1aa57df4d93edd33803}{\+::transpose}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of the transpose of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}


\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
If you want to replace a matrix by its own transpose, do {\bfseries{NOT}} do this\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}.transpose();\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ bug!!!\ caused\ by\ aliasing\ effect}}

\end{DoxyCode}
 Instead, use the \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac501bd942994af7a95d95bee7a16ad2a}{transpose\+In\+Place()} method\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}.transposeInPlace();}

\end{DoxyCode}
 which gives \doxylink{namespace_eigen}{Eigen} good opportunities for optimization, or alternatively you can also do\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}.transpose().eval();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac501bd942994af7a95d95bee7a16ad2a}{transpose\+In\+Place()}, \doxylink{adjoint_8cpp_a7333648f53414b05be9e4fd2f009fc22}{adjoint()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a38c0b074cf93fc194bf91141287cee3f}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!transpose@{transpose}}
\index{transpose@{transpose}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{transpose()}{transpose()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a38c0b074cf93fc194bf91141287cee3f} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a822af952eaf4205fd9ae3e54beb21146}{\+::\+Const\+Transpose\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abddae8e27995e1aa57df4d93edd33803}{\+::transpose}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

This is the const version of \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac8952c19644a4ac7e41bea45c19b909c}{transpose()}.

Make sure you read the warning for \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac8952c19644a4ac7e41bea45c19b909c}{transpose()} !

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac501bd942994af7a95d95bee7a16ad2a}{transpose\+In\+Place()}, \doxylink{adjoint_8cpp_a7333648f53414b05be9e4fd2f009fc22}{adjoint()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac501bd942994af7a95d95bee7a16ad2a}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!transposeInPlace@{transposeInPlace}}
\index{transposeInPlace@{transposeInPlace}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{transposeInPlace()}{transposeInPlace()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac501bd942994af7a95d95bee7a16ad2a} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::transpose\+In\+Place (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

This is the "{}in place"{} version of \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac8952c19644a4ac7e41bea45c19b909c}{transpose()}\+: it replaces {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} by its own transpose. Thus, doing 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}.transposeInPlace();}

\end{DoxyCode}
 has the same effect on m as doing 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}.transpose().eval();}

\end{DoxyCode}
 and is faster and also safer because in the latter line of code, forgetting the \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a5df64c66228ba75bbc66db2584185527}{eval()} results in a bug caused by \doxylink{group___topic_aliasing}{aliasing}.

Notice however that this method is only useful if you want to replace a matrix by its own transpose. If you just need the transpose of a matrix, use \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac8952c19644a4ac7e41bea45c19b909c}{transpose()}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
if the matrix is not square, then {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} must be a resizable matrix. This excludes (non-\/square) fixed-\/size matrices, block-\/expressions and maps.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_ac8952c19644a4ac7e41bea45c19b909c}{transpose()}, \doxylink{adjoint_8cpp_a7333648f53414b05be9e4fd2f009fc22}{adjoint()}, adjoint\+In\+Place() 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
the unique coefficient of a 1x1 expression 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a7f73df3954a09c7ab0dca208b6b23ddd}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!visit@{visit}}
\index{visit@{visit}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{visit()}{visit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a7f73df3954a09c7ab0dca208b6b23ddd} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Visitor$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::visit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Visitor \&}]{visitor}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Applies the visitor {\itshape visitor} to the whole coefficients of the matrix or vector.

The template parameter {\itshape Visitor} is the type of the visitor and provides the following interface\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }MyVisitor\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ called\ for\ the\ first\ coefficient}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{boing_8c_a2858154e2009b0e6e616f313177762bc}{init}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a052eb942d12b6404aade6fae4b075fb9}{Scalar}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{value}},\ Index\ \mbox{\hyperlink{_bi_c_g_s_t_a_b__step__by__step_8cpp_acb559820d9ca11295b4500f179ef6392}{i}},\ Index\ \mbox{\hyperlink{tut__arithmetic__redux__minmax_8cpp_a39513f0f8d942bf9ef17b2e87ac6d34e}{j}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ called\ for\ all\ other\ coefficients}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ operator()\ (\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a052eb942d12b6404aade6fae4b075fb9}{Scalar}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{value}},\ Index\ \mbox{\hyperlink{_bi_c_g_s_t_a_b__step__by__step_8cpp_acb559820d9ca11295b4500f179ef6392}{i}},\ Index\ \mbox{\hyperlink{tut__arithmetic__redux__minmax_8cpp_a39513f0f8d942bf9ef17b2e87ac6d34e}{j}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
compared to one or two {\itshape for} {\itshape loops}, visitors offer automatic unrolling for small fixed size matrix.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Zero()}{Zero()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a3832aa9b2ee9ebdb4458003c742c9027} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a3cb28fce3943b113439e17eef3c38552}{\+::\+Constant\+Return\+Type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Eigen\+::\+Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+Zero (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of a zero matrix.
\end{DoxyReturn}
The parameters {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} are the number of rows and of columns of the returned matrix. Must be compatible with this \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix_base}{Matrix\+Base} type.

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size matrix types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape rows} and {\itshape cols} as arguments, so \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors

This variant is meant to be used for dynamic-\/size vector types. For fixed-\/size types, it is redundant to pass {\itshape size} as argument, so \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a8c4be762b10041d64a2b2ce85bb14ba0}{Zero()} should be used instead.

\doxysubsection{友元及相关符号说明}
\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a3806d3f42de165878dace160e6aba40a}\index{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}!operator$<$$<$@{operator$<$$<$}}
\index{operator$<$$<$@{operator$<$$<$}!Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::DenseBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{operator$<$$<$()}{operator<<()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a3806d3f42de165878dace160e6aba40a} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
std\+::ostream \& operator$<$$<$ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::ostream \&}]{s}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$ \&}]{m}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [related]}}

Outputs the matrix, to the given stream.

If you wish to print the matrix with a format different than the default, use \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a148e20e32aa3ceca13e0a49c2cc584fc}{Dense\+Base\+::format()}.

It is also possible to change the default format by defining EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEFAULT\+\_\+\+IO\+\_\+\+FORMAT before including \doxylink{namespace_eigen}{Eigen} headers. If not defined, this will automatically be defined to \doxylink{struct_eigen_1_1_i_o_format}{Eigen\+::\+IOFormat()}, that is the \doxylink{struct_eigen_1_1_i_o_format}{Eigen\+::\+IOFormat} with default parameters.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base_a148e20e32aa3ceca13e0a49c2cc584fc}{Dense\+Base\+::format()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
